  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_7a9c177b-3f8b-42be-9472-a8ce9bf7c3d7'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();

<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<div class='spoiler'>
This answer contains spoilers…
<span class='spoilerAnswerText'>
<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  
    my guess is that Jennifer Parker was the one experiencing "rage of the angels" because she kept doing things that she knew, deep down inside that she <a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">…more</a>
    my guess is that Jennifer Parker was the one experiencing "rage of the angels" because she kept doing things that she knew, deep down inside that she shouldnt be doing; getting involved with a married man, working for the mafia, being involved with a man that she knew was bad news. In the end she can't be with the love of her life, her son dies, and she ends up all alone. Perhaps that is the rage of angels?<br /><br />Not sure, but that is all i can think of<a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">(less)</a>
  
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6194570342189942461">Rage of Angels, Sidney Sheldon <br/><br/>Rage of Angels is a novel by Sidney Sheldon published in 1980. As the story progresses, the protagonist is romantically torn between a famous politician, who helps her rise again, and the Mafia boss who framed her. The boss swears to destro</span>
  <span id="freeText6194570342189942461" style="display:none">Rage of Angels, Sidney Sheldon <br /><br />Rage of Angels is a novel by Sidney Sheldon published in 1980. The novel revolves around young attorney Jennifer Parker; as she rises as a successful lawyer, she gets into a series of on goings that lead to intrigue with the mob and a rival attorney that promises to break her life's dreams. As the story progresses, the protagonist is romantically torn between a famous politician, who helps her rise again, and the Mafia boss who framed her. The boss swears to destroy her after he finds out about her affair with the politician and the child resulting from the affair.<br /><br />تاریخ نخستین خوانش: روز هفدهم ماه جولای سال 1994 میلادی<br /><br />عنوان: خشم فرشتگان ؛ نویسنده: سیدنی شلدون؛ مترجم هادی عادلپور؛ تهران، کوشش، 1373؛ در 511ص؛ چاپ سوم 1379؛ چاپ پنجم 1388؛ شابک 9646326269؛ موضوع داستانهای نویسندگان امریکایی - سده 20م<br /><br />داستان دختری به نام «جنیفر پارکر» است؛ دختری که از ممتازترین شاگردان در دانشگاه حقوق بود؛ او سالهای طولانی و ملال آور را در دانشکده ی حقوق به پایان رساند، تا بالاخره به آرزوی دیرینه ی خود، که وکیل شدن بود، رسید؛ اما در نخستین روز حضورش در دادگاه، رویدادیی برای «جنیفر» افتاد، رخدادی ناباورانه، رویدادی که سرنوشت او را دیگر کرد؛ «جنیفر» در دام مافیا افتاد؛ و...؛ ا. شربیانی</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15070085126043309363">Amoung four <i>Sheldon</i>'s books, This one has to be my most fave!<br/><br/>The plot is so intense and unputdownable. <b>Jennifer Parker</b>, she is an intelligent associate, but her life turns up side down after she is choosen to be a pawn in the trial of a Mafia <b>Michael Moretti</b>.   <span id="freeText15070085126043309363" style="display:none">Amoung four <i>Sheldon</i>'s books, This one has to be my most fave!<br /><br />The plot is so intense and unputdownable. <b>Jennifer Parker</b>, she is an intelligent associate, but her life turns up side down after she is choosen to be a pawn in the trial of a Mafia <b>Michael Moretti</b>. She become notorious and no Law Firms accept her. But this strong girl never give up, she struggle and fight... and <i>This is the Story of the best Lawyer I've ever read.</i><br /><br />Gosh.. the Lawyer aspect of this book is even intenser than Julie James's books *no offence* I love her works anyway. BUT This is the Lawyer book I want to read! The books that I can experiance a lot of <b>
  <i>trials</i>
</b> in court. Sheldon is very well-written about the court scenes and I enjoy it that much. Nope, I love it! I found my heart beat fast several times and cried in some trial. <i>Jennifer</i> is such a smart clever lawyer I want to be.<br /><br /><b>Romance</b> is intense! <i>Jennifer</i> has to get involve romantically with two guys, an <i>Angel</i> and a <i>Demon</i>. Oh how I love the career of her love interests! <b>Adam Warner</b> is a smart Senator and <b>Michael Moretti</b> is a ruthless Mafia. Both handsome guys are powerful man who stay in the opposite sides and have to fight against each other in the politic game. *swoon*<br /><br />If you guys love reading about Lawyer, Politician, and Mafia.. Don't miss this book! That's all I want to say. :)</span>

  <span id="freeText12252973878550787086" style="display:none">After reading Rage of Angles, I am certain that I so much adore the girls who are independent, who love their freedom, who are not driven by what others tell them to do, who are on their own in this Jungle. <br /><br />I want to know what was not there in this book: love, hatred, agony, betrayal, intrigue, passion, just name it.<br /><br />Jennifer Parker, Adam Warner and Michael Moretti, I'm in love with these names.<br />I'm going to be terrified for the rest of my life with the last lines of this book --&gt; <br /><br />"But she was looking into the past, trying to understand when it was that all the laughter died."<br /><br />This is exactly what I felt after finishing it.<br />Just when I used to think that isn't everything going wonderful, that's a bit odd!   <span id="freeText9353640822710927346" style="display:none">Anatomy of a Sidney Sheldon read<br /><br />Upon getting book from library: I have read so many serious books lately. It'll be fun to read Sheldon again. I loved <i>Hart to Hart</i>. Cannot wait. <br /><br />Page 20: <i>another</i> virginal brilliant ingenue heroine? Oh well, at least this one is a lawyer<br /><br />page 31: well, that's actually a plausible setup for her losing her job with the DA's office<br /><br />page 104: seriously, she did NOT just turn to the jury in the middle of arguing a rule of evidence to deliver a lengthy soliloquy to them, did she? You so can't do that. <br /><br />Page 148: ok, make that another virginal brilliant ingenue heroine who falls in love with the wrong guy<br /><br />Page 175: you know, I liked <i>Hart to Hart</i> when I was 10.<br /><br />Page 200: How. Many. More. Pages?<br /><br />Page 205: time to start expediting this read<br /><br />Page 286: make that two wrong guys. And one of them reminds me a lot of <i>The Other side of Midnight</i>’s Larry Douglas mixed with Demiris.<br /><br />Page 420: this book is kinda sad <br /><br />Page 505: hooray I'm done. <br /><br />Verdict: maybe I'm too much of a literary snob to enjoy these sort of books anymore. Maybe if I were on an airplane. Still, way better than James Patterson. Sheldon really was a good storyteller for his genre and yet I wonder what he was trying to say. Stay virgins girls or you'll end up with a shady lady killer, literally? Or perhaps I overthink this.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer16333261328790710074">I read all Sidney’s stories, not including the last two books published. After knowing so many great books, I put Sidney Sheldon out of my priority.<br/>But from all the book he (I thought it was a she) wrote, this one and Sand of Times is my favourite.<br/>This book is about Jennifer (see, I still remember her name though I don’t have the book), a young lawyer who entered her career in a positive manner and optimism in her blood. But then many things happen and many people came along the way, that change</span>
  <span id="freeText16333261328790710074" style="display:none">I read all Sidney’s stories, not including the last two books published. After knowing so many great books, I put Sidney Sheldon out of my priority.<br />But from all the book he (I thought it was a she) wrote, this one and Sand of Times is my favourite.<br />This book is about Jennifer (see, I still remember her name though I don’t have the book), a young lawyer who entered her career in a positive manner and optimism in her blood. But then many things happen and many people came along the way, that changed her innocent way of thinking.<br />I found it scary, that people actually can change because of the situation happened to them.<br />I still feel my ‘crush’ on Michael Moretti (me and my best friend discuss about this guy a loooot) and reading about her boy –Joshua if I’m not mistaken- brought tears to my eyes.<br />I hate end of the story by the way. Her loneliness described very well, cause I felt a sting in my heart imagining her closing the door and trying to remember when was the last time she was happy. Hiks. I need end of Sands of Time to recover my sadness from reading this.<br /></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1482688211" />
    <a title="Hayat" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6116230-hayat"><img alt="Hayat" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420050859p2/6116230.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1482688211?book_show_action=true">Dec 27, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Hayat by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/10517119-pang">Pang</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6116230-hayat?shelf=big-books">big-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6116230-hayat?shelf=mystery-thriller">mystery-thriller</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6116230-hayat?shelf=heroine-independent-spirited">heroine-independent-spirited</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6116230-hayat?shelf=mishap-madness">mishap-madness</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6116230-hayat?shelf=antihero">antihero</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1482688211" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2598289009886317284"><b>This is my first Sidney Sheldon book and I love it</b><br/><br/>{Thank you Pang for recommending this book to me!}<br/><br/>I stayed awake all night to finish this amazing fast paced, multi-POV thriller with well developed plot full of interesting twists, great character development, brilliant cases with fascinating back stories. More importantly, I couldn't help admiring the main character, Jennifer Parker, a successful lawyer for sticking up for herself, for being such a fighter, a go-getter, a woman with talent, cou</span>
  <span id="freeText2598289009886317284" style="display:none"><b>This is my first Sidney Sheldon book and I love it</b><br /><br />{Thank you Pang for recommending this book to me!}<br /><br />I stayed awake all night to finish this amazing fast paced, multi-POV thriller with well developed plot full of interesting twists, great character development, brilliant cases with fascinating back stories. More importantly, I couldn't help admiring the main character, Jennifer Parker, a successful lawyer for sticking up for herself, for being such a fighter, a go-getter, a woman with talent, courage and intelligence who is not afraid to show it. At times, Jennifer was weak, she made stupid decisions that destroyed her hard work and reputation but then continued to follow up with more bad decisions concerning men, but that just makes her a deeply flawed interesting character and I like that. The ending was fitting and left space for possibilities. <br /><br />I really admire Sidney Sheldon for letting his main character go crazy, for not being afraid to let his heroine soar high, to be triumphant and suddenly fall to pieces in a major way that had me horrified. Usually, I don't like character devolution, but <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/43328.Rage_of_Angels" title="Rage of Angels by Sidney Sheldon" rel="nofollow noopener">Rage of Angels</a> was well done. I can't wait to try another Sidney Sheldon book. </span>

          </span>

<div id="review_211843863" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/211843863" />
    <a title="Asmita" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3736928-asmita"><img alt="Asmita" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/211843863?book_show_action=true">Sep 20, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Asmita" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Asmita" href="/user/show/3736928-asmita">Asmita</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3736928-asmita?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer211843863" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2978630897564088006">In Goodreads, a five star rating means that the book was really amazing, but Rage of Angels was not just amazing, it completely blew me away. Every author is so keen on making the leading character, a living legend, that the tragedy is lost. But that is the only emotion that we can relate to best apart from love. Joy is individual, sorrow is universal. Sidney Sheldon has pushed his imagination to the extremes, and finally there is everything in this book that a book needs to be complete.<br/><br/>Jennifer</span>
  <span id="freeText2978630897564088006" style="display:none">In Goodreads, a five star rating means that the book was really amazing, but Rage of Angels was not just amazing, it completely blew me away. Every author is so keen on making the leading character, a living legend, that the tragedy is lost. But that is the only emotion that we can relate to best apart from love. Joy is individual, sorrow is universal. Sidney Sheldon has pushed his imagination to the extremes, and finally there is everything in this book that a book needs to be complete.<br /><br />Jennifer is in love with Adam Warner and Michael Moretti and nothing seems to make sense and on top of that her son, Joshua, dies and she is all alone. Every author feels the need for adrenaline for his readers to enjoy his book to the fullest, but very few can actually display it in words. Everyone wants to play it safe, because no one wants the leading character to die or become the bad guy or change. But Sidney Sheldon had really shown what he can do with his characters. I love the ruthlessness in the writing. What happens to Jennifer in the book is what is likely to happen to a person sharing a fate similar to hers and no one can escape it. It’s easy for me to say because I don’t live her fate, but if I ever did, then I would be likely to feel the same conflicting emotion between Adam Warner, the person who stole her heart and created the loneliness in her life and Michael Moretti, the person who erased it and became the passion she could not resist. <br /><br />I would have felt much better if Joshua's death would have been framed by Michael’s mafia gang and then Jennifer would have gone against Michael while Michael was against her and Adam was against Michael. In that way, Jennifer would become Tracy Whitney (If Tomorrow Comes) for some time and then she could go back to living her normal life. But this is the only book that I have ever read that actually goes beyond the limitations of imagination and penetrates deeper into the tragedies of human life, which makes it much more believable as we can relate to it. <br /><br />Like every Shakespearean play ends with “All’s well that ends well”, every Sidney Sheldon novel ends with “If tomorrow comes, but tomorrow never does”. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2978630897564088006" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_216560006" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/216560006" />
    <a title="Luke Devenish" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4653034-luke-devenish"><img alt="Luke Devenish" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1332199117p2/4653034.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/216560006?book_show_action=true">Sep 28, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Luke Devenish" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Luke Devenish" href="/user/show/4653034-luke-devenish">Luke Devenish</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780688036874" href="/book/show/2460993.Rage_of_Angels">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer216560006" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9219895799029367126">Ah, Sidney, Sidney... I always come back to you when I need a bit of a palate cleanser between loftier fare. You never fail to entertain me. This time, though, you didn't quite electrify me. I don't think this is one of your best works. It's got some absolutely terrific elements (two thumbs up for the kid's near crucifixion; ditto for his water skiing horror), but somehow it just doesn't quite scale the giddy heights of excess that 'The Other Side of Midnight' does so very, very well. But this i</span>
  <span id="freeText9219895799029367126" style="display:none">Ah, Sidney, Sidney... I always come back to you when I need a bit of a palate cleanser between loftier fare. You never fail to entertain me. This time, though, you didn't quite electrify me. I don't think this is one of your best works. It's got some absolutely terrific elements (two thumbs up for the kid's near crucifixion; ditto for his water skiing horror), but somehow it just doesn't quite scale the giddy heights of excess that 'The Other Side of Midnight' does so very, very well. But this is not to say I wasn't gripped and engaged. I read this in a couple of days, which is doing very well for me. But some of the expectations I had in the excellent first half didn't quite deliver with pay-offs in the corruption-drenched second half. I REALLY hoped some of the clients Jennifer miraculously got off in her climb to the top would come back and save HER in the second half. They didn't. Not even poor Stumpy, the limbless beauty queen. Also, Ken...? Was he a pillow biting old Nancy or not? Admittedly my beat up 80s copy was missing ten pages around a third of the way in, but I doubt if those bits were crucial to the Ken subplot. What WAS Ken...? Anyway, even when faintly mediocre, Sidney is never boring. He continues to teach ME lessons about storytelling, and there are plenty of other writers with books on the shelves that I rather wish he'd teach as well.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9219895799029367126" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer16884653222444294211">I know this book was written in the early seventies and I tried really hard to keep that in context, but I just couldn't get past the rampant chauvanism this book was laden with. Sheldon tries to portray Jennifer Parker as a strong, independent woman but throughout the story, her life revolves around men! Her father dies of a broken heart after his wife's affair and subsequent abandonment...and his daughter proceeds to have not one but two relationships with married men! It just didn't jive. I f</span>
  <span id="freeText16884653222444294211" style="display:none">I know this book was written in the early seventies and I tried really hard to keep that in context, but I just couldn't get past the rampant chauvanism this book was laden with. Sheldon tries to portray Jennifer Parker as a strong, independent woman but throughout the story, her life revolves around men! Her father dies of a broken heart after his wife's affair and subsequent abandonment...and his daughter proceeds to have not one but two relationships with married men! It just didn't jive. I found very little to like about Jennifer. She was just so needy. But I think what I disliked most about Rage Of Angels was that by the end, it had turned me into a feminist (and now I realize 5 years later that I never hated feminism, I am a feminist, I only dislike the brand of feminism that strives to hate men for everything. )</span>

  <span id="freeText12124337077979539361" style="display:none">I'm not sure why is Sheldon against women in general, since I've read like only three books of his, but in both <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/43327.The_Sky_Is_Falling" title="The Sky Is Falling by Sidney Sheldon" rel="nofollow noopener">The Sky Is Falling</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/115130.A_Stranger_In_The_Mirror" title="A Stranger In The Mirror by Sidney Sheldon" rel="nofollow noopener">A Stranger In The Mirror</a> can be found a miserable and lonely woman that ends up exactly like that.       <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sully (thysaltymar)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sully (thysaltymar)" href="/user/show/9986049-sully-thysaltymar">Sully (thysaltymar)</a>

        rated it

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer586216013" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5358151541049384270">Beautifully written. Beautifully intensive.<br/><br/>This is another Sidney Sheldon novel that will take you off your seats, a real page-turner. A masterpiece. Another <b>Phenomenon</b>. If you remember his novel <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/43325.Nothing_Lasts_Forever' title='Nothing Lasts Forever by Sidney Sheldon' rel='nofollow noopener'>Nothing Lasts Forever</a> where it revolves around an intelligent doctor, now, the Rage of Angels tells the story of a young brilliant lawyer and anything that goes around the courtrooms. Rage if Angels is filled with love, tragedy, and a woman with two men. One of them is a good (white) angel, another is a</span>
  <span id="freeText5358151541049384270" style="display:none">Beautifully written. Beautifully intensive.<br /><br />This is another Sidney Sheldon novel that will take you off your seats, a real page-turner. A masterpiece. Another <b>Phenomenon</b>. If you remember his novel <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/43325.Nothing_Lasts_Forever" title="Nothing Lasts Forever by Sidney Sheldon" rel="nofollow noopener">Nothing Lasts Forever</a> where it revolves around an intelligent doctor, now, the Rage of Angels tells the story of a young brilliant lawyer and anything that goes around the courtrooms. Rage if Angels is filled with love, tragedy, and a woman with two men. One of them is a good (white) angel, another is a dark angel. <br /><br />The young intelligent attorney is Jennifer Parker, an attractive lady who lives in a cruel man's world, full of crimes, lies and murders, as she tremendously rises as a successful prominent lawyer in New York after being framed for threatening the District Attorney Robert De Silva who is the Chief executive against a Mafia boss, Michael Morreti which in turn leads to a situation that almost break her life's dreams. As the story progresses, our protagonist picked up every pieces of strength and dignity she still has in her and after having been successful in her <i>pro bono</i> cases she turns out to be the figure of the Godess of the courtrooms.<br /><br />If you are an aspiring lawyer or in the field of law, this is totally a book for you. You will learn several courtroom dialogues which might be useful for future Criminal Cases whether you are a Prosecutor or a Defense Counsel. You will also learn how to look into details in every possible (legit) way. <br /><br /><br />[..to be continued]</span>
  <a data-text-id="5358151541049384270" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer14470201602699252615">I read this book when I was in college. I think I still have it. Smart lawyer lady (Jennifer) gets involved with mob guy (Michael Moretti...I just loved that name) when she enlists his help to find her illigimate son (Fathered by a powerful congressman)who has been kidnapped by a lunatic who blames her for mishandling his case.<br/><br/>In return for Moretti's help, she becomes involved in a relationship with him.........all the while still being in love with her son's Father (the senator). <br/><br/>It's good vs. </span>
  <span id="freeText14470201602699252615" style="display:none">I read this book when I was in college. I think I still have it. Smart lawyer lady (Jennifer) gets involved with mob guy (Michael Moretti...I just loved that name) when she enlists his help to find her illigimate son (Fathered by a powerful congressman)who has been kidnapped by a lunatic who blames her for mishandling his case.<br /><br />In return for Moretti's help, she becomes involved in a relationship with him.........all the while still being in love with her son's Father (the senator). <br /><br />It's good vs. evil with Jennifer in the middle.<br /><br />This is one of the books. Probably considered a bit "low brow" but, I don't care........I loved it. Of course, that was almost 30 years ago. I might read (skim) it again and see if I feel the same way about it.</span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780062015570" href="/book/show/8181206-rage-of-angels">review of another edition</a>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/754607-nan?shelf=ebook">ebook</a>,

              <span id="reviewTextContainer109536588" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15691906562914453503">This is the first Sidney Sheldon novel I've read, and I can now understand why he's so popular.<br/><br/>Jennifer Parker is on her first day of her new job working for the District Attorney's office in New York City, when she does something horrible. She takes a package from a man in the courtroom and delivers it to the witness. She thinks the man works for her boss, but she's wrong. And the package contains a dead canary. With his Mafia trial falling apart once the witness refuses to continue his testimo</span>
  <span id="freeText15691906562914453503" style="display:none">This is the first Sidney Sheldon novel I've read, and I can now understand why he's so popular.<br /><br />Jennifer Parker is on her first day of her new job working for the District Attorney's office in New York City, when she does something horrible. She takes a package from a man in the courtroom and delivers it to the witness. She thinks the man works for her boss, but she's wrong. And the package contains a dead canary. With his Mafia trial falling apart once the witness refuses to continue his testimony, the district attorney vows to disbar Miss Parker. The defendant was Micheal Moretti, heir to one of New York's great Families.<br /><br />Weeks after the trial, Adam Warner steps into Parker's life. He's been asked to investigate her case for the disbarment hearing and to make a recommendation. People have political ambitions for Warner, and Parker's case is seen as a stepping stone for his great future.<br /><br />But nothing goes as planned. Moretti used Parker, and finds himself fascinated by her. Warner sees in her everything he's missing in his wife. The triangle between these three people will change their lives and the lives of everyone around them.<br /><br />The opening pages of the book are set in 1969, and it moves up to near the publication date of 1980. When I was reading the book, I had no idea that it was published thirty years ago. The writing felt vital and alive, and it was a powerful story. </span>
  <a data-text-id="15691906562914453503" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer544863062" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16272582980529434815">I love this book. Once this book was on my hand, I didn’t want to put it away. It was with me days and nights. I felt asleep reading it and in the morning, I would still find it, with page turned on where I left before involuntarily closing my eyes. This is the first book of Sidney Sheldon that made me cry. Once I started reading it, I was so deeply engrossed in it that I frequently lost the track of what’s happening around me. I wanted to finish it so quickly but at the same time, wished it wou</span>
  <span id="freeText16272582980529434815" style="display:none">I love this book. Once this book was on my hand, I didn’t want to put it away. It was with me days and nights. I felt asleep reading it and in the morning, I would still find it, with page turned on where I left before involuntarily closing my eyes. This is the first book of Sidney Sheldon that made me cry. Once I started reading it, I was so deeply engrossed in it that I frequently lost the track of what’s happening around me. I wanted to finish it so quickly but at the same time, wished it would never be finished. At some point, I just wished I were alone with this book. <br /><br />Another masterpiece of Sidney Sheldon; This is the story of Jennifer Parker, a lady with beauty and brain, who falls in love with two men from completely different background. One is the highly rated upcoming candidate of US president and another, the boss of the most powerful mafia organisation in the world. The story emphasizes on how Jennifer struggles around the strategized maze of vengeance, politics, love and crime. Jennifer faces injustice and betrayal that forces her to choose the path she didn’t want to. The part of her raising her son without his father knowing he ever had son with her is very emotional. Great finishing and attention to detail is mind blowing. <br /><br />I highly recommend this book to everyone. I definitely know that whenever I am alone and quiet, and its raining outside, I will be staring out of my window, with coffee in one hand and this book in another; refreshing each detail of the story, that has left enormous impact in my heart and brain. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16272582980529434815" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8178952713880934233">As soon as I started reading this one, I couldn't put it down.<br/><br/>The story focuses on Jennifer, a young idealist lawyer from a small town who has moved to the big city to put away the bad guys. After a major, albeit innocent, mistake she is completely outcast from her prosecutor's office and struggles to stay in the city and become a top lawyer.<br/><br/>I don't want to spoil too much more then that. I had no idea what I was getting into when I read this one and enjoyed the ride. I will warn you that this is</span>
  <span id="freeText8178952713880934233" style="display:none">As soon as I started reading this one, I couldn't put it down.<br /><br />The story focuses on Jennifer, a young idealist lawyer from a small town who has moved to the big city to put away the bad guys. After a major, albeit innocent, mistake she is completely outcast from her prosecutor's office and struggles to stay in the city and become a top lawyer.<br /><br />I don't want to spoil too much more then that. I had no idea what I was getting into when I read this one and enjoyed the ride. I will warn you that this is not a happy, feel-good book though, but it's very good and Sidney Sheldon has made my list of authors to check out. <br /><br />I highly recommend this book. </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('1mkkgzWKc/p2stNU8lgI2n49KI9qscJHtbC12RJvWXL2Cej6peNalfi6tu55tZQwBiE42q7XaTB7u19+j+JK2A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('QKdyVGmRSxUQP+q78L2kezkL/wqG0nXO2iqAe47WKKlgx74t+fhiep43jwF7UDiRQRfvX0K03rkUIWrcE1s7Aw==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer16170105353640831471">Sidney Sheldon (1917-2007) was an American writer who won awards in three careers—a Broadway playwright, a Hollywood TV and movie screenwriter, and a best-selling novelist.<br/><br/>His TV works spanned a twenty-year period during which he created <i>I Dream of Jeannie</i> (1965-70), <i>Hart to Hart</i> (1979-84), and <i>The Patty Duke Show</i> (1963-66), but it was not until after he turned 50 and began writing best-selling no</span>
  <span id="freeText16170105353640831471" style="display:none">Sidney Sheldon (1917-2007) was an American writer who won awards in three careers—a Broadway playwright, a Hollywood TV and movie screenwriter, and a best-selling novelist.<br /><br />His TV works spanned a twenty-year period during which he created <i>I Dream of Jeannie</i> (1965-70), <i>Hart to Hart</i> (1979-84), and <i>The Patty Duke Show</i> (1963-66), but it was not until after he turned 50 and began writing best-selling novels such as <i>Master of the Game</i> (1982), <i>The Other Side of Midnight</i> (1973) and <i>Rage of Angels</i> (1980) that he became most famous.</span>
